# Query 5: 59.18 QPS, 0.05x concurrency, ID 0xA2207B1E5D48A65E366B2D481D2D9508 at byte 2869369
# This item is included in the report because it matches --limit.
# Scores: V/M = 0.05

# Attribute    pct   total     min     max     avg     95%  stddev  median

# Lock time      3     7ms       0   390us     1us     1us     7us     1us
# Rows sent      1   3.58k       1       1       1       1       0       1
# Rows examine   0   3.58k       1       1       1       1       0       1
# Query size     0   1.60M     455     459  458.08  441.81       0  441.81
# String:
# Databases    isuconp
# Hosts        localhost
# Users        isuconp
# Query_time distribution
#   1us
#  10us
# 100us  ################################################################
#   1ms  #
#  10ms  #
# 100ms  #
#    1s
#  10s+
# Tables
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'posts'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`posts`\G
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'users'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`users`\G
# EXPLAIN /*!50100 PARTITIONS*/
SELECT
		posts.id AS post_id,
		posts.user_id AS post_user_id,
		posts.body AS post_body,
		posts.mime AS post_mime,
		posts.created_at AS post_created_at,
		users.account_name AS user_account_name,
		users.passhash AS user_passhash,
		users.authority AS user_authority,
		users.del_flg AS user_del_flg,
		users.created_at AS user_created_at
	FROM posts JOIN users
	ON users.id = posts.user_id
	WHERE posts.id = 3170
	ORDER BY posts.created_at DESC
	LIMIT 20\G

# Query 6: 13.68 QPS, 0.04x concurrency, ID 0x167A66FDC6782564234F598BDD504CEB at byte 2830914
# This item is included in the report because it matches --limit.
# Scores: V/M = 0.11
# Time range: 2023-11-05T10:37:39 to 2023-11-05T10:38:41
# Attribute    pct   total     min     max     avg     95%  stddev  median
# ============ === ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= =======
# Count          0     848
# Exec time      2      2s   169us   204ms     3ms     2ms    17ms   273us
# Lock time      0     2ms     1us    39us     1us     1us     2us     1us
# Rows sent      4   8.44k       2      20   10.20   15.25    3.08    9.83
# Rows examine   1   8.44k       2      20   10.20   15.25    3.08    9.83
# Query size     0 434.69k     524     525  524.91  511.45       0  511.45
# String:
# Databases    isuconp
# Hosts        localhost
# Users        isuconp
# Query_time distribution
#   1us
#  10us
# 100us  ################################################################
#   1ms  ###
#  10ms  #
# 100ms  #
#    1s
#  10s+
# Tables
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'posts'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`posts`\G
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'users'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`users`\G
# EXPLAIN /*!50100 PARTITIONS*/
SELECT
		posts.id AS post_id,
		posts.user_id AS post_user_id,
		posts.body AS post_body,
		posts.mime AS post_mime,
		posts.created_at AS post_created_at,
		users.account_name AS user_account_name,
		users.passhash AS user_passhash,
		users.authority AS user_authority,
		users.del_flg AS user_del_flg,
		users.created_at AS user_created_at
	FROM posts FORCE INDEX (user_id_created_at_index)
	JOIN users
	ON users.id = posts.user_id
	WHERE users.del_flg = 0
	AND posts.user_id = 271
	ORDER BY posts.created_at DESC
	LIMIT 20\G
